ee.openMenu = (e, t, n={}) => {
    const a = document.querySelector(`.${n.className || "generic-actions-menu"}`);
    a && a.remove();
    const s = d("div", {
        class: "context-menu"
    });
    n.className && s.classList.add(n.className),
    t.filter(e => !1 !== e.condition).forEach(e => {
        if (e.separator) {
            const e = d("div", {
                class: "context-menu-separator"
            });
            s.appendChild(e)
        }
        const t = d("div", {
            class: "context-menu-item"
        });
        e.danger && t.classList.add("danger");
        const n = d("span", {
            class: "context-menu-icon",
            html: e.icon
        })
          , a = d("span", {
            class: "context-menu-text",
            text: e.text
        });
        t.appendChild(n),
        t.appendChild(a),
        t.addEventListener("click", () => {
            s.remove(),
            e.action()
        }
        ),
        s.appendChild(t)
    }
    ),
    s.style.visibility = "hidden",
    document.body.appendChild(s);
    var i = e.getBoundingClientRect();
    const o = s.getBoundingClientRect()
      , r = n.offset || 5
      , l = window.innerWidth
      , c = window.innerHeight;
    s.style.zIndex = "900000",
    s.style.visibility = "visible";
    let u = i.left
      , h = i.top;
    switch (n.position) {
    case "bottom":
        u = i.left,
        h = i.bottom + r;
        break;
    case "left":
        u = i.left - o.width - r,
        h = i.top;
        break;
    case "right":
        u = i.right + r,
        h = i.top;
        break;
    case "top":
        u = i.left,
        h = i.top - o.height - r;
        break;
    case "center":
        u = i.left + i.width / 2 - o.width / 2,
        h = i.top + i.height / 2 - o.height / 2;
        break;
    default:
        u = i.left,
        h = i.top - o.height / 2
    }
    u + o.width > l && (u = l - o.width - 5),
    u < 5 && (u = 5),
    h + o.height > c && (h = c - o.height - 5),
    h < 5 && (h = 5),
    s.style.left = `${u}px`,
    s.style.top = `${h}px`;
    const p = t => {
        s.contains(t.target) || e.contains(t.target) || (s.remove(),
        document.removeEventListener("click", p),
        document.removeEventListener("scroll", p, !0))
    }
      , m = () => {
        s.remove(),
        document.removeEventListener("click", p),
        document.removeEventListener("scroll", m, !0)
    }
    ;
    setTimeout( () => {
        document.addEventListener("click", p),
        document.addEventListener("scroll", m, !0)
    }
    , 100)
}

const Le = class {
    static init() {
        if (this.tooltipElement)
            return;
        this.tooltipElement = d("div", {
            class: "wb-tooltip",
            style: {
                display: "none",
                zIndex: "999999"
            }
        }),
        document.body.appendChild(this.tooltipElement);
        const e = e => {
            Date.now() - this.lastShownTime < 100 || e.target.closest(".wb-tooltip") || this.hide()
        }
        ;
        document.addEventListener("mousedown", e, !0),
        document.addEventListener("touchstart", e, !0),
        window.addEventListener("resize", () => {
            this.viewportWidth = window.innerWidth,
            this.viewportHeight = window.innerHeight
        }
        )
    }
    static show(e, t, n) {
        if (this.tooltipElement || this.init(),
        !this.tooltipElement)

        }

    makeDraggable(e, t, n) {

          , s = 0
          , i = 0
          , o = 0
          , r = 0;

              , n = Math.max(0, t - this.baseExp);

    }
    static onExpUpdate(e) {
        if (!this.progress)
            return void (this.pendingExp = e);
        if (e <= this.baseExp)
            return;
        const t = e - this.baseExp
          , n = Math.min(this.progress.seasonXp, this.progress.earnedXp + t);

            return void (this.baseExp = e);

            this.progress.unclaimed++,

        this.baseExp = e,

    }

    }

        var e;

    static save() {
        if (e.saveTimer && (clearTimeout(e.saveTimer),
        e.saveTimer = null),
        I())
            return Promise.resolve();
        const t = Date.now();
        return (e.lastSaveTime ? t - e.lastSaveTime : 1 / 0) >= 5e3 ? e.saveImmediately() : new Promise(t => {
            e.saveTimer = setTimeout(async () => {
                await e.saveImmediately(),
                t()
            }
            , e.SAVE_DEBOUNCE_MS)
        }
        )
    }
    static async saveImmediately() {
        var t;
        if (0 !== Object.keys(e.pendingChanges).length) {
            this.lastSaveTime = Date.now();
            for (let a = 1; a <= 10; a++) {
                try {
                    const n = await li(oi.PLAYER, `/prefences/update?v=${null == (t = O.player) ? void 0 : t.id}`, {
                        method: "POST",
                        body: JSON.stringify({
                            prefs: e.pendingChanges
                        })
                    });
                    if (n.ok)
                        return e.lastSavedPrefs = {
                            ...e.lastSavedPrefs,
                            ...e.pendingChanges
                        },
                        void (e.pendingChanges = {});
                    if (n.status >= 400 && n.status < 500 && 429 !== n.status && 404 !== n.status)
                        return
                } catch (n) {}
                a < 10 && await new Promise(e => setTimeout(e, 8e3))
            }
        }
    }

Mt.EventBus = new class {
    constructor() {
        this.events = new Map
    }
    on(e, t) {
        this.events.has(e) || this.events.set(e, new Set),
        this.events.get(e).add(t)
    }
    off(e, t) {
        this.events.has(e) && (t ? this.events.get(e).delete(t) : this.events.delete(e))
    }
    emit(e, ...t) {
        if (this.events.has(e))
            for (const n of this.events.get(e))
                n(...t)
    }
}
